You can create a pre-written autoresponder email type&nbsp;and the submitter will get will the reply almost instantly.</p> \n<p>You can include a copy of the form data in the autoresponder email along with a PDF copy of the form responses.</p> \n<p>Here’s how you can configure the Google Forms addon to send autoresponder emails to the person who fills your Google Form.</p> \n<p>Open the Google Form, go to Addons &gt; Email Notifications &gt; Create Email Notification. If you run Mail Merge again, the row will be skipped and the&nbsp;email will not go out to recipients mentioned in that row.</p> \n<p><span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-wrapper\" style=\"position:relative;display:block;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;max-width:720px\"> <a class=\"gatsby-resp-image-link\" href=\"https://www.labnol.org/static/ae3629b111572ba48b7cb46a8062c0d2/e3d9b/mail-merge-status.png\" style=\"display:block\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"> <span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-background-image\" style=\"padding-bottom:17.22222222222222%;position:relative;bottom:0;left:0;background-image:url('data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAABQAAAADCAYAAACTWi8uAAAACXBIWXMAAAsSAAALEgHS3X78AAAAw0lEQVQI11WNjUoCURSE99kTBFPbFPyDUEtUtDRS1JKghzARUfa6K1x3VxFBhc2Iz6OB0cDAzJxhjjHXPreNGalnRaKpuK5ZmGdvEX+0iNUVmbZDrm2LPmWKbEuRfrGJVKeE7oeYtRHR8oCr4gBj5miSTYvSu0+x72E+KW7qEyofPnc9l0hlTEzK+Z6MdhZCTVVuhTeNKQ/DD5/ku85v/9XF8D2PYLvkD1/Cn4vbrTULeyIq4D8CDvsV+40Lh63473N6BCp0zJmUTwhpAAAAAElFTkSuQmCC');background-size:cover;display:block\"></span> <img class=\"gatsby-resp-image-image\" alt=\"mail-merge-status.png\" title=\"mail-merge-status.png\" src=\"https://www.labnol.org/static/ae3629b111572ba48b7cb46a8062c0d2/16546/mail-merge-status.png\" srcSet=\"/static/ae3629b111572ba48b7cb46a8062c0d2/96042/mail-merge-status.png 180w,/static/ae3629b111572ba48b7cb46a8062c0d2/7a322/mail-merge-status.png 360w,/static/ae3629b111572ba48b7cb46a8062c0d2/16546/mail-merge-status.png 720w,/static/ae3629b111572ba48b7cb46a8062c0d2/e3d9b/mail-merge-status.png 863w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 720px) 100vw, 720px\" style=\"width:100%;height:100%;margin:0;vertical-align:middle;position:absolute;top:0;left:0\" loading=\"lazy\" /> </a> </span></p> \n<p>Rows #4 and #5 will not be included in Mail Merge since the Mail Status column for these rows was&nbsp;manually set to SKIP</p> \n<p>Mail Merge status column can have 5 values:</p> \n<ol> \n <li><strong>Email Sent</strong> - The messages has been sent and this row will not be included in future merge until you clear the cell value.</li> \n <li><strong>Email Scheduled</strong> - The message is queued for future delivery. The status will auto change to Email Sent after the scheduled message is delivered.</li> \n <li><strong>Draft Created</strong> - If you are using Mail Merge to create drafts in Gmail, this status indicates that the draft has been created in Gmail for that recipient.</li> \n <li><strong>Quota Over</strong> - This indicates that you have&nbsp;run out of your daily email sending limit, new emails won’t be sent but you can still schedule messages.</li> \n <li><strong>Error Message</strong> - If merge encountered an error, maybe the email address was not valid, the status column will show the full error message.</li> \n</ol> \n<h3 id=\"how-to-skip-sending-mails-to-specific-rows\" style=\"position:relative\"><a 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>How to Skip Sending Mails to Specific Rows</h3> \n<p>Let’s say you have a Google Spreadsheet with a dozen&nbsp;entries but you would only like to include, say, 5 rows in&nbsp;Mail Merge and skip the other rows.</p> \n<p>You can easily do this by manually setting the Mail Merge Status column as SKIP for rows that you would not like to be included in the merge.</p> \n<p>Also, rows with status as “Email Sent” will also not included in the merges.</p> \n<h2 id=\"use-google-sheets-filters-to-hide-rows\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/email-specific-rows-7131#use-google-sheets-filters-to-hide-rows\" aria-label=\"use google Google Sheets Filters to Hide Rows</h2> \n<p>Mail Merge for Gmail will only send emails to rows that are visible (not hidden) in your Google Sheet. If you are using Filters inside Google Sheets to hide rows that don’t meet a certain criteria, the emails will not be sent to the hidden rows.</p> \n<p>Say you have a Google Sheet with hundreds of rows and the column titles are Name, Country, Age and Email Address.&nbsp;You would only like to send emails to rows where the Country is United States and Age &gt; 18 years.</p> \n<p>All you have to do is create a filter inside Google Spreadsheet with the specified criteria and all the unmatched rows will be hidden. Mail merge will automatically skip the rows hidden by the Google Sheets filter.</p> \n<p><strong>Step 1:</strong> Select the Data Range, go to Data and Choose Filter.</p> \n<p><span Configure Document Template</h4> \n<p>Go to the Document Merge section and select the template you created in the previous step. to the Form Submitter</strong></p> \n<p>Suppose you have a question - <em>Email Address</em> - in your Google Form where you ask the submitter to provide their email address. people submit your Google Form, a new row is inserted in the Google Sheet that is storing the form responses. This spreadsheet row contains a Timestamp column, the actual date when the form was submitted, and the other columns in the sheet contain all the user’s answers, one per column.</p> \n<p>You can extend the Google Forms sheet to also include formula fields and the cell values are automatically calculated whenever a new row is added to the sheet by the Google Form. For instance:</p> \n<ul> \n <li>You can have an auto-number formula that assigns an auto-incrementing but sequential ID to every form response. It can be useful when you are using Google Forms for <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=PBN9SaG-MJQ&amp;list=PLIO7o3VwD0X-Fv9Ooe46iGMKzgPWGR8qG&amp;index=2\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">invoicing</a>.</li> \n <li>For customer order forms, a formula can be written in Google Sheets to calculate the total amount based on the item selection, the country (tax rates are different) and the quantity selected in the form.</li> \n <li>For hotel reservations forms, a formula can automatically calculate the room rent based on the check-in and check-out date filled by the customer in the Google Form.</li> \n <li>For quizzes, a teacher can automatically calculate the final score of the student by matching the values entered in the form with the actual answers and assigning scores.</li> \n <li>If a users has made multiple form submissions, a formula can help you determine the total number of entries made by a user as soon as they submit a form.</li> \n</ul> style=\"width:100%;height:100%;margin:0;vertical-align:middle;position:absolute;top:0;left:0\" loading=\"lazy\" /> </a> </span></p> \n<h3 id=\"google-sheets-formulas-for-google-forms\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/google-form-formulas-050520#google-sheets-formulas-for-google-forms\" aria-label=\"google sheets formulas for google forms permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Google Sheets Formulas for Google Forms</h3> \n<p>In this step by step guide, you’ll learn how to add formulas to Google Sheets that are associated with Google Forms. The corresponding cell values in the response rows will be automatically calculated when a new response is submitted.</p> \n<p>To get a better understanding of what we are trying to achieve, open this <a href=\"https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLScgXeCkFPqhFcTO-S0KjEmeLZvnV2_oB7mQrMPaSZeJXsSgYg/viewform?usp=sf_link\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Google Form</a> and submit a response. Next, open this <a href=\"https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1RQ6K_6U68NUChi0PhUeyYADhOskbwh3fe_mpUXMA8oU/edit#gid=1364341769\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Google Sheet</a> and you’ll find your response in a new row. The columns F-K are autofilled using formulas.</p> \n<p>All examples below will use the <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/arrayformula-copy-formulas-in-entire-column/29711/\">ArrayFormula</a> function of Google Sheets though some of these example can also be written using the <code class=\"language-text\">FILTER</code> function.</p> \n<h4 id=\"auto-number-form-responses-with-a-unique-id\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/google-form-formulas-050520#auto-number-form-responses-with-a-unique-id\" aria-label=\"auto number form responses with a unique id permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Auto-Number Form Responses with a Unique ID</h4> \n<p>Open the Google Sheet that is storing form responses, go to first empty column and copy-paste the following formula in the row #1 of the empty column.</p> \n<div class=\"gatsby-highlight\" data-language=\"text\"> \n <pre class=\"language-text\"><code class=\"language-text\">=ArrayFormula(\n  IFS(\n    ROW(A:A)=1, \"Invoice ID\",\n    LEN(A:A)=0, IFERROR(1/0),\n    LEN(A:A)&gt;0, LEFT(CONCAT(REPT(\"0\",5), ROW(A:A) -1),6)\n  )\n)</code></pre> \n</div> \n<p>The <code class=\"language-text\">ROW()</code> function returns the row number of the current response row. It returns <code class=\"language-text\">1</code> for the first row in the Invoice Column and thus we set the column title in the first row. For subsequent rows, if the first column of the row (usually Timestamp) is not empty, the invoice ID is auto generated.</p> \n<p>The IDs will be like <code class=\"language-text\">00001</code>, <code class=\"language-text\">00002</code> and so on. You only need to place the formula is first row of the column and it auto-populates all the other rows in the column.</p> \n<p>The <code class=\"language-text\">IFERROR</code> function returns the first argument if it is not an error value, otherwise returns the second argument if present, or a blank if the second argument is absent. So in this case <code class=\"language-text\">1/0</code> is an error and thus it always returns a blank value.</p> \n<h4 id=\"date-calculation-formula-for-google-forms\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/google-form-formulas-050520#date-calculation-formula-for-google-forms\" aria-label=\"date calculation formula for google forms permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Date Calculation Formula for Google Forms</h4> \n<p>Your Google Form has two date fields - the check-in date and the check-out date. The hotel rates may vary every season so you have a separate table in the Google Sheet that maintains the room rent per month.</p> \n<p><span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-wrapper\" style=\"position:relative;display:block;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;max-width:679px\"> <a class=\"gatsby-resp-image-link\" href=\"https://www.labnol.org/static/7be579e937c8037b309ade1b5a36029e/ba204/google-sheets-formula.png\" style=\"display:block\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"> <span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-background-image\" style=\"padding-bottom:57.22222222222223%;position:relative;bottom:0;left:0;display:block\"></span> <img class=\"gatsby-resp-image-image\" alt=\"Google Sheets Date Formula\" title=\"Google Sheets Date Formula\" src=\"https://www.labnol.org/static/7be579e937c8037b309ade1b5a36029e/ba204/google-sheets-formula.png\" srcSet=\"/static/7be579e937c8037b309ade1b5a36029e/96042/google-sheets-formula.png 180w,/static/7be579e937c8037b309ade1b5a36029e/7a322/google-sheets-formula.png 360w,/static/7be579e937c8037b309ade1b5a36029e/ba204/google-sheets-formula.png 679w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 679px) 100vw, 679px\" style=\"width:100%;height:100%;margin:0;vertical-align:middle;position:absolute;top:0;left:0\" loading=\"lazy\" /> </a> </span></p> \n<p>The Column C in the Google Sheet holds the responses for the check-in date while the D column is storing the check-out dates.</p> \n<div class=\"gatsby-highlight\" data-language=\"text\"> \n <pre class=\"language-text\"><code class=\"language-text\">=ArrayFormula(\n    IF(ROW(A:A) = 1,\n      \"Room Rent\",\n      IF(NOT(ISBLANK(A:A)),\n       (D:D - C:C) *\n       VLOOKUP(MONTH(D:D), 'Room Rates'!$B$2:$C$13,2, TRUE),\n       \"\"\n      )\n   )\n)</code></pre> \n</div> \n<p>The formulas uses <code class=\"language-text\">VLOOKUP</code> to get the room rates for the travel date specified in the form response and then calculates the room rent by multiplying the room rent with duration of stay.</p> \n<p>The same formula can also be written with <code class=\"language-text\">IFS</code> instead of <code class=\"language-text\">VLOOKUP</code></p> \n<div class=\"gatsby-highlight\" data-language=\"text\"> \n <pre class=\"language-text\"><code class=\"language-text\">=ArrayFormula(\n    IF(ROW(A:A) = 1,\n        \"Room Rent\",\n        IFS(ISBLANK(C:C), \"\",\n           MONTH(C:C) &lt; 2, 299,\n           MONTH(C:C) &lt; 5, 499,\n           MONTH(C:C) &lt; 9, 699,\n           TRUE, 199\n        )\n    )\n)</code></pre> \n</div> \n<h4 id=\"calculate-tax-amount-based-on-invoice-value\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/google-form-formulas-050520#calculate-tax-amount-based-on-invoice-value\" aria-label=\"calculate tax amount based on invoice value permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Calculate Tax Amount Based on Invoice Value</h4> \n<p>In this approach, we’ll use the <code class=\"language-text\">FILTER</code> function and that could lead to a less complicated formula than using using <code class=\"language-text\">IF</code> function. The downside is that you have to write the column title in row #1 and paste the formulas in row #2 (so one form response should exist for the formula to work).</p> \n<div class=\"gatsby-highlight\" data-language=\"text\"> \n <pre class=\"language-text\"><code class=\"language-text\">=ArrayFormula(FILTER(E2:E, E2:E&lt;&gt;\"\")*1.35)</code></pre> \n</div> \n<p>Here we apply 35% tax to the invoice value and this formula should be added in the row #2 of the column titled “Tax Amount” as shown in the screenshot.</p> \n<h4 id=\"assign-quiz-scores-in-google-forms\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/google-form-formulas-050520#assign-quiz-scores-in-google-forms\" aria-label=\"assign quiz scores in google forms permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Assign Quiz Scores in Google Forms</h4> \n<p>Which city is known as the big apple? This is a short-answer question in Google Forms so students can give responses like New York, New York City, NYC and they’ll still be correct. The teacher has to assign 10 points to the correct answer.</p> \n<div class=\"gatsby-highlight\" data-language=\"text\"> \n <pre class=\"language-text\"><code class=\"language-text\">=ArrayFormula(\n    IF(ROW(A:A) = 1,\n      \"Quiz Score\",\n      IFS(\n        ISBLANK(A:A), \"\",\n        REGEXMATCH(LOWER({B:B}), \"new\\s?york\"), 10,\n        {B:B} = \"NYC\", 10,\n        TRUE, 0\n      )\n    )\n)</code></pre> \n</div> \n<p>In this formula, we are making use of the <code class=\"language-text\">IFS</code> function that like an <code class=\"language-text\">IF THEN</code> statement in <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/learn-coding-online/28537/\">programming</a>. We are using <code class=\"language-text\">REGEXMATCH</code> to match values like <code class=\"language-text\">New York, New York, newyork</code> in one go using <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/regular-expressions-forms/28380/\">regular expressions</a>.</p> \n<p>The <code class=\"language-text\">IFS</code> function returns an <code class=\"language-text\">NA</code> if none of the conditions are true so we add a <code class=\"language-text\">TRUE</code> check at the end that will always be evaluated to <code class=\"language-text\">true</code> if none of the previous conditions matched and returns <code class=\"language-text\">0</code>.</p> \n<h4 id=\"extract-the-first-name-of-the-form-respondent\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/google-form-formulas-050520#extract-the-first-name-of-the-form-respondent\" aria-label=\"extract the first name of the form respondent permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Extract the First Name of the Form Respondent</h4> \n<p>If you have form field that asks the user to entire their full name, you can use Google Sheets function to extract the first name from the full name and use that field to <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/personalized-mail-merge-in-gmail/20981/\">send personalised emails</a>.</p> \n<div class=\"gatsby-highlight\" data-language=\"text\"> \n <pre class=\"language-text\"><code class=\"language-text\">=ArrayFormula(\n  IFS(\n    ROW(A:A)=1, \"First Name\",\n    LEN(A:A)=0, IFERROR(1/0),\n    LEN(A:A)&gt;0, PROPER(REGEXEXTRACT(B:B, \"^[^\\s+]+\"))\n  )\n)</code></pre> \n</div> \n<p>We’ve used <code class=\"language-text\">RegexExtract</code> method here to fetch the string before the first space in the name field. The <code class=\"language-text\">PROPER</code> function will capitalise the first letter of the name incase the user entered their name in lower case.</p> \n<h4 id=\"find-duplicate-google-form-submissions\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/google-form-formulas-050520#find-duplicate-google-form-submissions\" aria-label=\"find duplicate google form submissions permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Find Duplicate Google Form Submissions</h4> \n<p>If your Google Form is collection email addresses, you can use that field to quickly detect responses that have been submitted by the same user multiple times.</p> \n<div class=\"gatsby-highlight\" data-language=\"text\"> \n <pre class=\"language-text\"><code class=\"language-text\">=ArrayFormula(\n  IFS(\n    ROW(A:A)=1, \"Is Duplicate Entry?\",\n    LEN(A:A)=0, IFERROR(1/0),\n    LEN(A:A)&gt;0, IF(COUNTIF(B:B, B:B) &gt; 1, \"YES\", \"\")\n  )\n)</code></pre> \n</div> \n<p>Assuming that the Column B is storing the email addresses of the form respondents, we can use the <code class=\"language-text\">COUNTIF</code> function to quickly mark duplicate entries in our responses spreadsheet. You can also use <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/alternate-color-rows-in-google-sheets/28701/\">conditional formatting</a> in Sheets to highlight rows that are possible duplicate entries.</p> \n<h4 id=\"email-form-responses-with-autofill-values\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/google-form-formulas-050520#email-form-responses-with-autofill-values\" aria-label=\"email form responses with autofill values permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Email Form Responses with AutoFill Values</h4> \n<p>You can use <a href=\"https://gsuite.google.com/marketplace/app/document_studio/429444628321\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Document Studio</a> to automatically send an email to the form respondents. The email is sent after the formular values are auto-filled by the Google Sheet. The original form response and the calculated values can also be included in the generated <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/generate-pdf-files-from-google-forms-6324\">PDF document</a>.</p> \n<p><iframe width=\"100%\" height=\"315\" src=\"https://www.youtube-nocookie.com/embed/TSDXfdo3JVU?rel=0\" frameBorder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe></p>","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Tue, 05 May 2020 15:17:38 +0000","feedId":259,"bgimg":"https://www.labnol.org/static/f164b514f4056e99eb2a6e55cf3f427c/16546/google-forms-formula.png","linkMd5":"c8b9783c7f333ab0893fe38bed0732ad","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx/cdn7@2020_6/2020/08/16/10-30-16-442_63436619f6498236.webp","destWidth":720,"destHeight":496,"author":"","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://www.labnol.org/static/f164b514f4056e99eb2a6e55cf3f427c/16546/google-forms-formula.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn53@2020_3/2020/08/16/10-30-16-438_63436619f6498236.webp","https://www.labnol.org/static/7be579e937c8037b309ade1b5a36029e/ba204/google-sheets-formula.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx11/cdn52@2020_6/2020/08/16/10-30-18-561_554bf97381813349.webp"}},{"createdTime":"2020-08-16 18:29:53","updatedTime":"2020-08-16 18:29:53","title":"How to Change the Reply-To Email Address in Google Form Notifications","link":"https://www.labnol.org/change-reply-email-address-7278","description":"<p>The Reply-To email address is the address where the emails go when someone replies to your email notification generated by the <a href=\"https://gsuite.google.com/marketplace/app/email_notifications_for_google_forms/984866591130\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Google Forms addon</a>.</p> \n<p>By default, the reply to address is set the email address of the form owner so all replies to form notifications emails are sent to them. You can, however, use any other email address in the reply to field.</p> \n<h2 id=\"how-to-set-reply-to-email-in-google-forms\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/change-reply-email-address-7278#how-to-set-reply-to-email-in-google-forms\" aria-label=\"how to set reply to email in google forms permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>How to Set Reply To Email in Google Forms</h2> \n<p>Go to the Google Forms, choose Add-ons and then Email Notifications. You can either create a new email notification rule or edit an existing notification.</p> \n<p><span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-wrapper\" style=\"position:relative;display:block;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;max-width:627px\"> <a class=\"gatsby-resp-image-link\" the reply to field where you would like the replies to go. You should include only a single email address and it must be a valid email.</p> \n<h3 id=\"send-replies-to-form-respondent\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/change-reply-email-address-7278#send-replies-to-form-respondent\" aria-label=\"send replies to form respondent permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Send Replies to Form Respondent</h3> \n<p><strong>Change the reply to address to go to the form submitter’s email</strong></p> \n<p>It is also possible to have the form submitter’s email address in the reply to field. This is useful because you can respond to the form submitter by simply replying to the notification email without having to manually change the email in the To: box.</p> \n<p>To edit the reply-to email address and set it to the respondent’s email address, <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/edit-email-notifications-forms-10908\">edit the notification</a> and put the {{Email Question}} in the reply to field. For instance, if your form question is “Your email”, you should put {{Your email}} in the reply-to field and.</p> \n<p>The template variable in double curly braces will be replaced with the actual email address filled by the user when they were submitting the form. srcSet=\"/static/ce107aad99467119180f8dd3d0910363/96042/public-toilet-location-google-maps.png 180w,/static/ce107aad99467119180f8dd3d0910363/7a322/public-toilet-location-google-maps.png sizes=\"(max-width: 720px) 100vw, 720px\" style=\"width:100%;height:100%;margin:0;vertical-align:middle;position:absolute;top:0;left:0\" loading=\"lazy\" /> </a> </span></p> \n<p>If you are traveling in a new location, the public toilets and bathroom finder option avaialble inside Google Maps could come in very handy.</p> \n<p>Open the Google Maps on your phone (or open maps.google.com on your desktop browser), make sure that the location services are turned on and type the query <code class=\"language-text\">public toilets near me</code>.</p> \n<p>Google Maps will instantly show you the location of restrooms near your current location.</p> \n<p>The feature also works inside Google Assistant. Say “OK Google” to activate the Assistant, say the command “Show me toilets near me” and it will open maps with placemarkers for all the toilets near your location.</p> \n<p>If location is unavailale on your phone, or if you wish to learn about restroom in a particular location without actually being there, change your search query to use the address instead of <code class=\"language-text\">near me</code>.</p> \n<p>Your query in that case will be <code class=\"language-text\">show toilets near Taj Mahal in Agra</code> or <code class=\"language-text\">Public Restrooms in Times Square</code> or <code class=\"language-text\">Where can I find a bathroom in NYC</code>.</p> \n<p>In India alone, more than 57k toilets and restrooms in urban India can be found through Google Maps. formatting and parsing dates. Here are some sample formats and the corresponding outut.</p> \n<table> \n <thead> \n  <tr> \n   <th>Date Format</th> \n   <th>Sample Output</th> \n  </tr> \n </thead> \n <tbody> \n  <tr> \n   <td>yyyy-MM-d hh:mm a</td> \n   <td>2016-11-28 06:30 PM</td> \n  </tr> \n  <tr> \n   <td>yyyy-MMM-d HH:mm:ss</td> \n   <td>2016-Nov-28 18:30:22</td> \n  </tr> \n  <tr> \n   <td>EEE, d MMM yyyy</td> \n   <td>Wed, 4 Jul 2016</td> \n  </tr> \n  <tr> \n   <td>yyyy/MM/dd HH:mm:ss</td> \n   <td>2016/11/29 12:08:56</td> \n  </tr> \n </tbody> \n</table> \n<p>“M” represents the month in year. You can say “MMMM” to output the full name of the month.</p> \n<p>Similarly, “E” is day name of the week while “a” is the AM / PM marker. 18:29:53","updatedTime":"2020-08-16 18:29:53","title":"How to Use Template {{Markers}} in Document Studio","link":"https://www.labnol.org/template-markers-6086","description":"<p>Your Document Studio templates can include any variable field that is available as a column title in the Google Sheet. In case of Google Forms, you can use any question title as your marker and the marker should be exactly as your question title enclosed in double curly braces.</p> \n<p>For instance, if a question in your Google Form says “What is your name”, the marker you’ll use in your document template will be <code class=\"language-text\">{{What is your name}}</code>.</p> \n<p>You can also create additional columns in the source Google Spreadsheet with formulas and use them as dynamic markers in your Google template. Let me show you an example.</p> \n<p>Create a new column and call it <strong>Row Number</strong>. Now go to the first empty cell of that column and put this <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/arrayformula-copy-formulas-in-entire-column/29711/\">ArrayFormula function</a>:</p> \n<div class=\"gatsby-highlight\" data-language=\"text\"> \n <pre class=\"language-text\"><code class=\"language-text\">=ArrayFormula(if(LEN(A2:A);&nbsp;row(A2:A) -1;))</code></pre> \n</div> \n<p>What we have added a column that displays the row number of the rows and we can now put <code class=\"language-text\">{{Row Number}}</code> in your document templates, merged file names and Drive folder path. For instance, if you put <code class=\"language-text\">Invoice #{{Row Number}}</code> in the file name, the files name would be named Invoice #1, Invoice #2 and so on automatically.</p> \n<h3 id=\"formatting-date-and-time\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/template-markers-6086#formatting-date-and-time\" aria-label=\"formatting date and time permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Formatting Date and Time</h3> \n<p>The same technique can be used to format date and time information for including in your templates.</p> \n<p>Say the first column in your Google Sheet in called Timestamp and it includes the date and time when a Google Form response was submitted. Add a new column called Submission Time and add this formula in the first empty cell.</p> \n<div class=\"gatsby-highlight\" data-language=\"text\"> \n <pre class=\"language-text\"><code class=\"language-text\">=ArrayFormula(if(NOT(ISBLANK(A2:A)),HOUR(A2:A)&amp;\":\"&amp;MINUTE(A2:A),))</code></pre> \n</div> \n<p>You can now include the submission time in your email and document template using the <code class=\"language-text\">{{Submission Time}}</code> variable field.</p> \n<h2 id=\"standard-markers-for-google-forms\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/template-markers-6086#standard-markers-for-google-forms\" aria-label=\"standard markers for google forms permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Standard Markers for Google Forms</h2> \n<p>In addition to standard form questions and column headers, Google Forms also support a few standard markers like:</p> \n<ul> \n <li><strong>{{Response Number}}</strong>&nbsp;- Form Response number</li> \n <li><strong>{{Form Name}}</strong>&nbsp;- The name of the Google Form</li> \n <li><strong>{{Form Url}}</strong>&nbsp;- A link to the associated Google Form</li> \n <li><strong>{{Response Id}}</strong>&nbsp;- Unique response ID generated by Google Form</li> \n <li><strong>{{Response Url}}</strong>&nbsp;- Directly link to view / edit the current form submission</li> \n <li><strong>{{Response Date}}</strong>&nbsp;- The full timestamp when a form was submitted</li> \n <li><strong>{{Respondent Email}}</strong>&nbsp;- If your Google Form is capturing email addresses, this will include the email address of the form respondent.</li> \n <li><strong>{{All Markers}}</strong> - An HTML table containing all the form responses in a neat tabular format.</li> \n</ul> \n<p>You should put <code class=\"language-text\">{{All Answers}}</code> in your email body to receive a copy of the form answers in an email notification.</p>","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Tue, 27 Aug 2019 If you require technical help, the app may ask you to share your add-on settings with the developer for support.</li> \n <li>The app will not store your data on non-Google servers. All your settings are stored on Google servers inside the property store of the Google project associated with the addon.</li> \n <li>The app will not use any of your data for market research, advertising, serving personalized content, retargeting, or recommendations.</li> \n <li>The App will only use access to Gmail to send emails on your behalf and will not use your data for any other purpose.</li> \n <li>We will not transfer or share your information with others&nbsp;unless doing so is necessary to provide and improve these features, comply with applicable law, or as part of a merger, acquisition, or sale of assets.</li> \n</ul> \n<p>Google sign-in will authenticate your identity and provide you the option to share certain personal information with us such as your email address. The information you provide is held in strict confidence. We collect this information to generate your user license, send payment receipts and communicate with the user about product updates.</p> \n<p>If your personal information changes, or if you no longer desire our service, you may delete or deactivate it by uninstalling our Google add-on or by contacting us. Internally, when a form is submitted, a trigger is invoked that uses the Gmail API to send email messages on your behalf. The trigger works in real-time and the notifications are sent instantly.</p> \n<p>If you are not receiving email notifications, here are some troubleshooting tips.</p> \n<h3 id=\"1-check-your-email-folders\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/forms-notifications-troubleshoot-7299#1-check-your-email-folders\" aria-label=\"1 check your email folders permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>1. Check your Email Folders</h3> \n<p>Open your Google Form, submit a test response and then go to the Sent Items folder of your Gmail account. A copy of all email notifications is automatically saved in your Gmail mailbox. Also, check the Spam folder of the recipient’s mailbox. Sometimes an email may get marked as junk due to the message content.</p> \n<h3 id=\"2-is-your-email-quota-over\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/forms-notifications-troubleshoot-7299#2-is-your-email-quota-over\" aria-label=\"2 is your email quota over permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>2. Is your Email Quota Over?</h3> \n<p>Free users can send up to 20 form responses per day while premium users can email up to 400 - 1500 recipients per 24 hours. Google Apps for Work, G Suite and Google Apps for Education users can send up to 1500 email recipients with the premium edition.</p> \n<p>The <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/google-forms-email-limit-7283\">daily email limit</a> is <strong>email recipients per day</strong> and not email messages per day. Thus if you are emailing a single&nbsp;form&nbsp;response to 2 people, it will reduce your daily quota by 2. Gmail counts every email in the To, CC or BCC field as a separate email (even if they are part of the same message) and thus counts towards your quota.</p> \n<p>Google will automatically reset your daily email limit at midnight Pacific Time.</p> \n<h3 id=\"3-is-gmail-enabled-for-your-google-apps-domain\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/forms-notifications-troubleshoot-7299#3-is-gmail-enabled-for-your-google-apps-domain\" aria-label=\"3 is gmail enabled for your google apps domain permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>3. Is Gmail Enabled for your Google Apps domain</h3> \n<p>If you are Google Apps / G Suite user, your domain admin needs to enable the Gmail service for you to send email messages through any of the <a href=\"https://digitalinspiration.com\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Google Add-ons</a>. See <a href=\"https://support.google.com/a/answer/57919\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">this link</a> for steps on how to enable the Gmail service for users in your organization.</p> \n<h3 id=\"4-are-you-getting-multiple-email-notifications\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/forms-notifications-troubleshoot-7299#4-are-you-getting-multiple-email-notifications\" aria-label=\"4 are you getting multiple email notifications permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>4. Are you Getting Multiple Email Notifications</h3> \n<p>It is likely that your Google Form is shared with multiple people. If they too have configured the Email Notifications add-on, the emails will go out from their email account resulting in duplicate emails.</p> \n<p>To rectify the issue, open the Google Form, go to add-ons &gt; Email Notifications, Troubleshooting and choose <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/disable-email-notifications-7265\">Disable Notifications</a>. You need to do this under the email account that is sending the duplicate email notification.</p> \n<h3 id=\"5-logged-into-multiple-google-accounts\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/forms-notifications-troubleshoot-7299#5-logged-into-multiple-google-accounts\" aria-label=\"5 logged into multiple google accounts permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>5. Logged into Multiple Google Accounts</h3> \n<p>Google Forms add-on may not work if you are logged into multiple Google accounts in the same browser.</p> \n<p>If you are unable to add or edit rules inside the Google Forms addon, try logging out of all the other Google Account. Alternatively, open Google Chrome, go to the menu and choose New Incognito Window. Here open the same Google Form and try editing the rule.</p> \n<h3 id=\"6-cookies-are-blocked-in-your-browser\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/forms-notifications-troubleshoot-7299#6-cookies-are-blocked-in-your-browser\" aria-label=\"6 cookies are blocked in your browser permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>6. Cookies are Blocked in your Browser.</h3> \n<p>The Google Forms add-on requires you to ensure that third-party cookies are not blocked in your browser.</p> \n<p>Please see this guide on <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/enable-third-party-cookies-in-google-chrome-14986\">how to enable cookies</a>.</p> \n<h3 id=\"5-restart-google-form-notifications\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/forms-notifications-troubleshoot-7299#5-restart-google-form-notifications\" aria-label=\"5 restart google form notifications permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>5. can choose to send a notification to the parent if the age entered is less than 18. If you are using Google Forms for tech support, you can choose to send an email notification to the manager if the customer has picked “high” for&nbsp;the severity level.</p> \n<p>Conditional or rule-based notifications in Google Forms can also be used to send an email notification to different people based on answers. For instance,&nbsp;you can set the&nbsp;notifications to go to <a href=\"mailto:apple@example.com\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">apple@example.com</a> only if the user has put&nbsp;iPhone or iPad&nbsp;in the product list.</p> \n<h3 id=\"set-up-notification-emails-based-on-conditions\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/send-conditional-emails-7290#set-up-notification-emails-based-on-conditions\" aria-label=\"set up notification emails based on conditions permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Set up Notification Emails Based on Conditions</h3> \n<p>In this tutorial, we’ll explain how to set up notification emails that are trigger based on the form response. We would like the notifications to go out if the entered country is India <strong>OR</strong>&nbsp;if the email address contains ctrlq.org.</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://www.labnol.org/4d8028be312b9f9404d9fb4a371b7834/google-forms-conditional-emails.gif\" alt=\"google-forms-conditional-emails.gif\" /></p> \n<p>Open the Google Form, go to Add-ons &gt; Email Notifications for Forms &gt; Create a new Email Notification. In the Specify Condition screen, choose “Match Any (OR)” since we need to trigger then email when either of the conditions is met.</p> \n<p>Next choose “Country” in the “Select Field” drop-down, set the match&nbsp;type as “Equals” and the matching value as India. Similarly, add a condition for “Email Address” and set the match type as “Contains” as shown below.</p> \n<p>Save the rule. If either of the conditions is met, the notifications are sent and the form entry is saved. If the conditions are not met, the notification email is skipped while the submitted&nbsp;data is still saved in your form.</p> \n<h3 id=\"advanced-filters-in-google-forms\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/send-conditional-emails-7290#advanced-filters-in-google-forms\" aria-label=\"advanced filters in google forms permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Advanced Filters in Google Forms</h3> \n<p>The Google Forms add-on lets you easily create advanced filters with multiple criteria. Here are some examples.</p> \n<p><span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-wrapper\" style=\"position:relative;display:block;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;max-width:654px\"> <a class=\"gatsby-resp-image-link\" href=\"https://www.labnol.org/static/92849b39c1b1e4773f8810df8bfd531e/8179f/form-test-conditions.png\" style=\"display:block\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"> <span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-background-image\" style=\"padding-bottom:70%;position:relative;bottom:0;left:0;display:block\"></span> <img class=\"gatsby-resp-image-image\" alt=\"form-test-conditions.png\" title=\"form-test-conditions.png\" src=\"https://www.labnol.org/static/92849b39c1b1e4773f8810df8bfd531e/8179f/form-test-conditions.png\" srcSet=\"/static/92849b39c1b1e4773f8810df8bfd531e/96042/form-test-conditions.png 180w,/static/92849b39c1b1e4773f8810df8bfd531e/7a322/form-test-conditions.png 360w,/static/92849b39c1b1e4773f8810df8bfd531e/8179f/form-test-conditions.png 654w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 654px) 100vw, 654px\" style=\"width:100%;height:100%;margin:0;vertical-align:middle;position:absolute;top:0;left:0\" loading=\"lazy\" /> </a> </span></p> \n<h4 id=\"for-text-fields\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/send-conditional-emails-7290#for-text-fields\" aria-label=\"for text fields permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>For Text Fields</h4> \n<ul> \n <li>Equals - Answer&nbsp;exactly matches the specified text</li> \n <li>Contains - Text is anywhere inside the answer field</li> \n <li>Does not contain - Answer does not contain the specified text</li> \n <li>Any of - Specify a list of values (comma separated) and the answer should be one of these values</li> \n <li>None of - Answer should not equal to any item in the list (comma separated)</li> \n <li>Is Empty - The answer is blank</li> \n <li>Is Not Empty - The answer contains at least one character (not blank)</li> \n</ul> \n<h4 id=\"for-numeric-fields\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/send-conditional-emails-7290#for-numeric-fields\" aria-label=\"for numeric fields permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>For Numeric Fields</h4> \n<ul> \n <li>Equal to - Answer matches the specified numeric value</li> \n <li>Not Equal to - Answer doesn’t match the number</li> \n <li>Greater than - Answer is greater or equal to number</li> \n <li>Less than - Answer is less or equal to number</li> \n</ul> \n<p><em><strong>Tip:</strong> If you would like to check if an answer is between two numbers, create two conditions for the same field - greater than the lower limit and lower than the upper limit.</em></p> \n<h4 id=\"regular-expressions\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/send-conditional-emails-7290#regular-expressions\" aria-label=\"regular expressions permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Regular Expressions</h4> \n<p>Advanced users may apply <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/learn-regular-expressions/28841/\">regular expressions</a> to match answers against patterns. For instance, if you would like to send email notifications only when the city field contains exactly 4 characters, the regex value would be <em>^.{4}$</em> (case insensitive by default).&nbsp;A regex like (iPad|iPhone|Mac|Macbook) would match any Apple product.</p> \n<h3 id=\"match-all-conditions-or-any\" style=\"position:relative\"><a Who is the host of this website? Which mail service is this domain using? There exist <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/tools/best-online-tools-for-webmasters-know-everything-about-websites/2744/\">web tools</a> that can uncover these details but this sort of research can also be done using the command line on your computer.</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://www.labnol.org/7ce581e63aac3303f6003979e6e51260/network-commands.gif\" alt=\"Network Commands\" /></p> \n<p>Let’s explore a few essential networking commands that will help you know everything about a website from the terminal itself.</p> \n<h3 id=\"what-is-my-ip-address\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/network-commands-200706#what-is-my-ip-address\" aria-label=\"what is my ip address permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>What is my IP address</h3> \n<div class=\"gatsby-highlight\" data-language=\"bash\"> \n <pre class=\"language-bash\"><code class=\"language-bash\"><span class=\"token function\">curl</span> https://checkip.amazonaws.com</code></pre> \n</div> \n<p>Make a curl or <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/software/wget-command-examples/28750/\">wget</a> request to the <code class=\"language-text\">checkip.amazonaws.com</code> and it prints the public IP address of your computer. You can also connect to Akamai’s <code class=\"language-text\">whatismyip.akamai.com</code> domain get your external IP address.</p> \n<h3 id=\"what-is-my-private-ip-address\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/network-commands-200706#what-is-my-private-ip-address\" aria-label=\"what is my private ip address permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>What is my Private IP address</h3> \n<div class=\"gatsby-highlight\" data-language=\"bash\"> \n <pre class=\"language-bash\"><code class=\"language-bash\"><span class=\"token function\">ifconfig</span> en0 <span class=\"token operator\">|</span> <span class=\"token function\">grep</span> inet</code></pre> \n</div> \n<p>Your computer has a private IP address that only work within the local network. For older Macs with a wired Ethernet port, use en0 for Ethernet interface or en1 for the WiFi interface. The <code class=\"language-text\">networksetup -listnetworkserviceorder</code> command will print a list all network interfaces available on your machine.</p> \n<h3 id=\"find-the-location-of-ip-address\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/network-commands-200706#find-the-location-of-ip-address\" aria-label=\"find the location of ip address permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Find the Location of IP address</h3> \n<div class=\"gatsby-highlight\" data-language=\"bash\"> \n <pre class=\"language-bash\"><code class=\"language-bash\"><span class=\"token function\">curl</span> https://ip2c.org/?ip<span class=\"token operator\">=</span><span class=\"token number\">8.8</span>.8.8</code></pre> \n</div> \n<p>The free ‘ip2c’ service resolves an IP address to the country.</p> \n<p>Or use the ‘ipapi’ service to get more details of an IP address including the city name, timezone and even the latitude and longitude associated with an IP address.</p> \n<div class=\"gatsby-highlight\" data-language=\"bash\"> \n <pre class=\"language-bash\"><code class=\"language-bash\"><span class=\"token function\">curl</span> https://ipapi.co/8.8.8.8/json</code></pre> \n</div> \n<h3 id=\"check-dns-records\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/network-commands-200706#check-dns-records\" aria-label=\"check dns records permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Check DNS Records</h3> \n<p>The <code class=\"language-text\">dig</code> command will help you query for any type of DNS records for a domain from the command line.</p> \n<h4 id=\"1-find-the-ip-address-of-a-website\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/network-commands-200706#1-find-the-ip-address-of-a-website\" aria-label=\"1 find the ip address of a website permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>1. Find the IP address of a website</h4> \n<div class=\"gatsby-highlight\" data-language=\"bash\"> \n <pre class=\"language-bash\"><code class=\"language-bash\"><span class=\"token function\">dig</span> +short www.labnol.org</code></pre> \n</div> \n<h4 id=\"2-find-the-mail-server-of-domain\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/network-commands-200706#2-find-the-mail-server-of-domain\" aria-label=\"2 find the mail server of domain permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>2. Find the Mail Server of Domain</h4> \n<p>The Mail Exchange (MX) records specify the incoming mail servers that used for delivering email messages sent to your domain name.</p> \n<div class=\"gatsby-highlight\" data-language=\"bash\"> \n <pre class=\"language-bash\"><code class=\"language-bash\"><span class=\"token function\">host</span> -t MX labnol.org</code></pre> \n</div> \n<h4 id=\"3-print-all-dns-records-of-a-domain\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/network-commands-200706#3-print-all-dns-records-of-a-domain\" aria-label=\"3 print all dns records of a domain permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>3. Print all DNS Records of a Domain</h4> \n<p>Get a list of all DNS records of a domain including TXT records, MX records and name servers. The name servers handle queries regarding the location of the domain’s website, email and other services.</p> \n<div class=\"gatsby-highlight\" data-language=\"bash\"> \n <pre class=\"language-bash\"><code class=\"language-bash\"><span class=\"token function\">dig</span> +nocmd amazon.com any +noall +answer</code></pre> \n</div> \n<h3 id=\"who-is-hosting-a-website\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/network-commands-200706#who-is-hosting-a-website\" aria-label=\"who is hosting a website permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Who is hosting a website?</h3> \n<p>Use the <code class=\"language-text\">dig</code> command to find the IP address of a website and then use the same dig command to perform a reverse lookup to find the host of that IP address.</p> \n<p>For instance, this command will print the IP address of the Netflix website:</p> \n<div class=\"gatsby-highlight\" data-language=\"bash\"> \n <pre class=\"language-bash\"><code class=\"language-bash\"><span class=\"token function\">dig</span> +short netflix.com A <span class=\"token operator\">|</span> <span class=\"token function\">tail</span> -1</code></pre> \n</div> \n<p>Use that IP address in the next command to get the hostname:</p> \n<div class=\"gatsby-highlight\" data-language=\"bash\"> \n <pre class=\"language-bash\"><code class=\"language-bash\"><span class=\"token function\">dig</span> +nocmd -x <span class=\"token number\">52.11</span>.104.17 +noall +answer</code></pre> \n</div> \n<h3 id=\"find-the-owner-of-the-website\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/network-commands-200706#find-the-owner-of-the-website\" aria-label=\"find the owner of the website permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Find the owner of the website</h3> \n<p>Use the built-in <code class=\"language-text\">whois</code> command to reveal important information about any web domain including the date when it was first registered, the contact details of the website owner, the expiration date of the domain, the name of the domain registrar and so on.</p> \n<div class=\"gatsby-highlight\" data-language=\"bash\"> \n <pre class=\"language-bash\"><code class=\"language-bash\">whois dictation.io</code></pre> \n</div> \n<p>You can also query the domain registration details on a specific registrar’s server with the <code class=\"language-text\">-h</code> flag. For instance, the next command performs a whois lookup on a website using the WHOIS server of <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/google-domains-review/30355/\">Google Domains</a>.</p> \n<div class=\"gatsby-highlight\" data-language=\"bash\"> \n <pre class=\"language-bash\"><code class=\"language-bash\">whois -h whois.google.com reverse.photos</code></pre> \n</div> \n<h3 id=\"test-network-connectivity-with-ping\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/network-commands-200706#test-network-connectivity-with-ping\" aria-label=\"test network connectivity with ping permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Test Network Connectivity with Ping</h3> \n<p>The ping command helps you test if a remote host is reachable and whether your machine can connect to it properly.</p> \n<div class=\"gatsby-highlight\" data-language=\"bash\"> \n <pre class=\"language-bash\"><code class=\"language-bash\"><span class=\"token function\">ping</span> -c <span class=\"token number\">5</span> -i <span class=\"token number\">2</span> labnol.org</code></pre> \n</div> \n<p>The above command pings the host 5 time and there’s a 2 second wait between pings.</p> \n<h3 id=\"wheres-the-fault\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/network-commands-200706#wheres-the-fault\" aria-label=\"wheres the fault permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Where’s the fault?</h3> \n<p>If your Internet connection is working but you are unable to reach a website, there could be an issue with an intermediate router that the packets have to pass through to reach the server.</p> \n<p>The <code class=\"language-text\">traceroute</code> commands prints the network path from your local computer to the website that the traffic must pass through and this information can be useful for diagnosing connectivity issues.</p> \n<div class=\"gatsby-highlight\" data-language=\"bash\"> \n <pre class=\"language-bash\"><code class=\"language-bash\"><span class=\"token function\">traceroute</span> labnol.org</code></pre> \n</div> \n<p>Also see: <a Cookies are considered “bad” as they are mostly used for tracking users on the Internet but some cookies serve a useful purpose as well.</p> \n<p>For instance, a <a href=\"https://digitalinspiration.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">GSuite add-on</a> may open a small sidebar inside Google Sheets and this sidebar may need to communicate with other windows that are opened by the same add-on. Since the windows are on different domains, the only way for them to communicate with each other is through third-party cookies.</p> \n<p>This video explains why some <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=jFmPHPmTDeM\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">third-party cookies</a> are necessary and how you can selectively allow cookies inside Google Chrome.</p> \n<p><iframe width=\"100%\" height=\"315\" src=\"https://www.youtube-nocookie.com/embed/jFmPHPmTDeM?rel=0\" frameBorder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; This will only allow cookies for GSuite add-ons in Google Sheets, Form, Docs, and Google Sides.</p> \n<p><strong>Step 1:</strong> Open Google Chrome browser, click the settings menu in the top right (3 vertical dots).</p> \n<p><span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-wrapper\" style=\"position:relative;display:block;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;max-width:720px\"> <a class=\"gatsby-resp-image-link\" 18:29:53","updatedTime":"2020-08-16 18:29:53","title":"How to Send Google Forms Email Notifications from Another Email Address (Alias)","link":"https://www.labnol.org/change-sender-email-7275","description":"<p>Email Notifications in Google Forms, by default, are sent on behalf of the email address of the Google Account that owns the Google Form. For instance, if my Gmail email&nbsp;address is <a href=\"mailto:forms@google.com\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">forms@google.com</a> and I create a new Google Form, the sender’s email in the outgoing message will be listed as <a href=\"mailto:forms@google.com\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">forms@google.com</a>.</p> \n<p>You can, however, use an alternative email address as the default sender for your Google Forms emails.</p> \n<p>This is particularly useful in organizations where the person managing the form is not the same as the person who owns the form. Or if you have created your Google Form under your personal Google Account but would like to send emails on behalf of your work email.</p> \n<h3 id=\"send-google-form-emails-from-another-address\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/change-sender-email-7275#send-google-form-emails-from-another-address\" aria-label=\"send google form emails from another address permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Send Google Form Emails from Another Address</h3> \n<p>To get started, go to your Gmail account, choose Settings, Accounts and choose “Add another email address” in the “Send Mail As” section.</p> \n<p>Here enter your name and the alternate email address that you would like to send the Google Forms emails from.&nbsp;Make sure the “Treat as alias” option is checked else the Gmail API may not treat the new email as a valid alias of your account.</p> \n<p><span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-wrapper\" style=\"position:relative;display:block;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;max-width:570px\"> <a class=\"gatsby-resp-image-link\" The email messages are sent&nbsp;through your Gmail account and there are&nbsp;certain sending limits on the number of email messages you can send per day through Google Forms.</p> \n<p>The email sending limits for Google Forms vary based on the type of your Gmail or G Suite / Google Apps account and is defined as the maximum number of emails you can send in a 24-hour period. The email quota resets automatically around midnight PST.</p> \n<p>All free users of the Google Forms add-on can send up to 20 form responses per day. Please note that this sending limit is&nbsp;based on “email recipients per day” rather than on&nbsp;form responses. &nbsp;Thus, if you are sending a form notification to 2 people, the form owner, and the form respondent, it will reduce your daily quota by 2 as there are 2 recipients even though a single form response was received.</p> \n<h2 id=\"google-forms---email-sending-limit\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/google-forms-email-limit-7283#google-forms---email-sending-limit\" aria-label=\"google forms   email sending limit permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Google Forms - Email Sending Limit</h2> \n<p>This table compares the email sending limit of Google Forms per 24-hour period based on the type of your Google Account. The limits are dependent on which G Suite edition you have.</p> \n<table> \n <thead> \n  <tr> \n   <th>Google Account</th> \n   <th>Free Email Limit</th> \n   <th>Premium Email Limit</th> \n  </tr> \n </thead> \n <tbody> \n  <tr> \n   <td>Gmail Accounts</td> \n   <td>20</td> \n   <td>400</td> \n  </tr> \n  <tr> \n   <td>G Suite Legacy (Free Google Apps)</td> \n   <td>20</td> \n   <td>400</td> \n  </tr> \n  <tr> \n   <td>G Suite Basic, GSuite Business, GSuite Education, GSuite Enterprise</td> \n   <td>20</td> \n   <td>1500</td> \n  </tr> \n </tbody> \n</table> \n<p><strong>PS:</strong> If you have recently&nbsp;upgraded your free Gmail or Google Apps account to G Suite Business, Google may put your email account in trial mode for few billing cycles. During this period, your premium limit will be similar to G Suite Basic users.</p> \n<h3 id=\"what-happens-when-you-reach-your-daily-sending-limit\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/google-forms-email-limit-7283#what-happens-when-you-reach-your-daily-sending-limit\" aria-label=\"what happens when you reach your daily sending limit permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>What Happens When You Reach your Daily Sending Limit</h3> \n<p>When your daily email limit is reached, the email notifications will be suspended&nbsp;until Google resets your limit within the 24-hour period. The notifications will resume when the quota is reset.</p> \n<p>However, if your Google Form has received any new response in the period when your email quota was unavailable, no notifications would go out to that respondent.</p> \n<p>All email notifications sent through your Google Form are also saved in the sent items folder of your Gmail account. You can view the sent emails to know if any form responses were not auto-responded.</p> \n<p>You can either:</p> \n<ol> \n <li>Upgrade to the premium version and instantly increase your daily email sending limit</li> \n <li>If you are a premium user already, you can <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/resend-email-notifications-7285\">resend email notifications</a> to respondents manually.</li>
